  private FullToken forceNext() {
    var tk = lexer.next();
    precededBySemicolon = false;
    while (tk == Token.LINE_COMMENT
        || tk == Token.BLOCK_COMMENT
        || tk == Token.SEMICOLON
        || tk == Token.SHEBANG) {
      precededBySemicolon = precededBySemicolon || tk == Token.SEMICOLON;
      tk = lexer.next();
    }
    return new FullToken(tk, lexer.span(), lexer.newLinesBetween);
  }

    return prev;

  private void backtrack() {
    assert !backtracking;
    lookahead = prev.token;
    spanLookahead = prev.span;

  private void ensureEmptyHeaders(MemberHeader header, String messageArg) {
    if (header.isNotEmpty()) {
      throw new ParserError(
          ErrorMessages.create("wrongHeaders", messageArg), header.span(spanLookahead));
    }
  }

  public Parser() {}

  private void init(String source) {
    this.lexer = new Lexer(source);
    _lookahead = forceNext();
    lookahead = _lookahead.token;
    spanLookahead = _lookahead.span;
  }

  public Module parseModule(String source) {
    init(source);
    if (lookahead == Token.EOF) {
      return new Module(Collections.singletonList(null), new Span(0, 0));
    }
    var start = spanLookahead;
    Span end = null;
    ModuleDecl moduleDecl;
    var nodes = new ArrayList<Node>();
    try {
      var header = parseMemberHeader();

      moduleDecl = parseModuleDecl(header);
      if (moduleDecl != null) {
        end = moduleDecl.span();
        header = null;
      }
      nodes.add(moduleDecl);
      // imports
      while (lookahead == Token.IMPORT || lookahead == Token.IMPORT_STAR) {
        if (header != null && header.isNotEmpty()) {
          throw parserError("wrongHeaders", "Imports");
        }
        var _import = parseImportDecl();
        nodes.add(_import);
        end = _import.span();
      }

      // entries
      if (header != null && header.isNotEmpty()) {
        end = parseModuleMember(header, nodes);
      }

      while (lookahead != Token.EOF) {
        header = parseMemberHeader();
        end = parseModuleMember(header, nodes);
      }
      return new Module(nodes, start.endWith(spanLookahead));
    } catch (ParserError pe) {
      var spanEnd = end != null ? end : start;
      pe.setPartialParseResult(new Module(nodes, start.endWith(spanEnd)));
      throw pe;
    }
  }

  public Expr parseExpressionInput(String source) {
    init(source);
    var expr = parseExpr();
    expect(Token.EOF, "unexpectedToken", "end of file");
    return expr;
  }

  public ReplInput parseReplInput(String source) {
    init(source);
    var nodes = new ArrayList<Node>();
    while (lookahead != Token.EOF) {
      var header = parseMemberHeader();
      switch (lookahead) {
        case IMPORT, IMPORT_STAR -> {
          ensureEmptyHeaders(header, "Imports");
          nodes.add(parseImportDecl());
        }
        case MODULE, AMENDS, EXTENDS -> nodes.add(parseModuleDecl(header));
        case CLASS -> nodes.add(parseClass(header));
        case TYPE_ALIAS -> nodes.add(parseTypeAlias(header));
        case FUNCTION -> nodes.add(parseClassMethod(header));
        case IDENTIFIER -> {
          next();
          switch (lookahead) {
            case COLON, ASSIGN, LBRACE -> {
              backtrack();
              nodes.add(parseClassProperty(header));
            }
            default -> {
              backtrack();
              ensureEmptyHeaders(header, "Expressions");
              nodes.add(parseExpr());
            }
          }
        }
        default -> {
          ensureEmptyHeaders(header, "Expressions");
          nodes.add(parseExpr());
        }
      }
    }
    Span span;
    if (nodes.isEmpty()) {
      span = new Span(0, 0);
    } else {
      span = nodes.get(0).span().endWith(nodes.get(nodes.size() - 1).span());

OBSERVATION:

  // Like next, but don't ignore comments
  private FullToken nextComment() {
    prev = _lookahead;
    _lookahead = forceNextComment();
    lookahead = _lookahead.token;
    spanLookahead = _lookahead.span;
    return prev;
  }

  private FullToken forceNextComment() {
    var tk = lexer.next();
    precededBySemicolon = false;
    while (tk == Token.SEMICOLON) {
      precededBySemicolon = true;
      tk = lexer.next();
    }
    return new FullToken(tk, lexer.span(), lexer.newLinesBetween);
  }

  private FullToken forceNext() {
    var tk = lexer.next();
    precededBySemicolon = false;
    while (tk == Token.LINE_COMMENT
        || tk == Token.BLOCK_COMMENT
        || tk == Token.SEMICOLON
        || tk == Token.SHEBANG) {
      precededBySemicolon = precededBySemicolon || tk == Token.SEMICOLON;
      tk = lexer.next();
    }
    return new FullToken(tk, lexer.span(), lexer.newLinesBetween);
  }

      }
      case '/' -> lexSlash();
      case '"' -> lexStringStart(0);
      case '#' -> {
        if (lookahead == '!') {
          yield lexShebang();
        } else {
          yield lexStringStartPounds();
        }
      }
      default -> {
        if (Character.isDigit(ch)) {
          yield lexNumber(ch);
        } else if (isIdentifierStart(ch)) {

  private Token nextString() {
    var scope = interpolationStack.getFirst();
    if (stringEnded) {
      lexStringEnd(scope);
      stringEnded = false;
      interpolationStack.pop();
      state = State.DEFAULT;
      return Token.STRING_END;
    }
    if (lookahead == EOF) return Token.EOF;
    if (isEscape) {
      isEscape = false;
      // consume the `\#*`
      for (var i = 0; i < scope.pounds + 1; i++) {
        nextChar();
      }
--
      nextChar();
      lexExponent();
    }
  }

  private Token lexShebang() {
    do {
      nextChar();
    } while (lookahead != '\n' && lookahead != '\r' && lookahead != EOF);
    return Token.SHEBANG;
  }

  private boolean isHex(char ch) {
    var code = (int) ch;
    return (code >= 48 && code <= 57) || (code >= 97 && code <= 102) || (code >= 65 && code <= 70);
  }

  private static boolean isIdentifierStart(char c) {
    return c == '_' || c == '$' || Character.isUnicodeIdentifierStart(c);
  }

  private static boolean isIdentifierPart(char c) {
    return c != EOF && (c == '$' || Character.isUnicodeIdentifierPart(c));
  }

  private char nextChar() {
    var tmp = lookahead;
    cursor++;
    if (cursor >= size) {
      lookahead = EOF;
    } else {
      lookahead = source[cursor];
    }
    return tmp;
  }

1. Track whether we're at the beginning of the file/parsing

  private FullToken forceNext() {
    var tk = lexer.next();
    precededBySemicolon = false;
    while (tk == Token.LINE_COMMENT
        || tk == Token.BLOCK_COMMENT
        || tk == Token.SEMICOLON
        || tk == Token.SHEBANG) {
      precededBySemicolon = precededBySemicolon || tk == Token.SEMICOLON;
      tk = lexer.next();
    }
    return new FullToken(tk, lexer.span(), lexer.newLinesBetween);
  }

  // Like next, but don't ignore comments
  private FullToken nextComment() {
    prev = _lookahead;

I need to implement the fix for the shebang parsing issue. The problem is that the `forceNext()` method in `Parser.java` treats `SHEBANG` tokens like regular comments and semicolons, allowing them to be skipped anywhere in the file. However, according to the PR description, shebangs should only be valid at the very beginning of the file.

Let me create a Python script to make the necessary changes to the Parser.java file:

import re

# Read the original Parser.java file

    content = f.read()

pattern = r'"'"'(private boolean precededBySemicolon = false;)'"'"'
new_content = re.sub(pattern, r'"'"'\1\n  private boolean atBeginning = true;'"'"', content)

# Modify the init method to reset atBeginning
pattern = r'"'"'(private void init\(String source\) {\n    this\.lexer = new Lexer\(source\);\n    _lookahead = forceNext\(\);)'"'"'
new_content = re.sub(pattern, r'"'"'\1\n    atBeginning = false;'"'"', new_content)

# Modify the forceNext method to check for shebang at the beginning
pattern = r'"'"'(private FullToken forceNext\(\) {\n    var tk = lexer\.next\(\);\n    precededBySemicolon = false;)'"'"'
replacement = r'"'"''"'"''"'"'\1
    
    // Shebang should only be allowed at the beginning of the file
    if (!atBeginning && tk == Token.SHEBANG) {
      throw parserError("shebangNotAtBeginning");
    }
    '"'"''"'"''"'"'

    f.write(new_content)

  private FullToken forceNext() {
    var tk = lexer.next();
    precededBySemicolon = false;

    // Shebang should only be allowed at the beginning of the file
    if (!atBeginning && tk == Token.SHEBANG) {
      throw parserError("shebangNotAtBeginning");
    }

    // Shebang should only be allowed at the beginning of the file
    if (!atBeginning && tk == Token.SHEBANG) {
      throw parserError("shebangNotAtBeginning");
    }

    while (tk == Token.LINE_COMMENT
        || tk == Token.BLOCK_COMMENT
        || tk == Token.SEMICOLON
        || tk == Token.SHEBANG) {
      precededBySemicolon = precededBySemicolon || tk == Token.SEMICOLON;
      tk = lexer.next();
    }

  private FullToken forceNext() {
    var tk = lexer.next();
    precededBySemicolon = false;
    
    // Shebang should only be allowed at the beginning of the file
    if (!atBeginning && tk == Token.SHEBANG) {
      throw parserError("shebangNotAtBeginning");
    }

        || tk == Token.BLOCK_COMMENT
        || tk == Token.SEMICOLON
        || tk == Token.SHEBANG) {

      tk = lexer.next();

package org.pkl.parser.util;

import java.text.MessageFormat;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.ResourceBundle;

public final class ErrorMessages {
  private ErrorMessages() {}

  public static String create(String messageName, Object... args) {
    var locale = Locale.getDefault();
    var errorMessage =
        ResourceBundle.getBundle("org.pkl.parser.errorMessages", locale).getString(messageName);

    // only format if `errorMessage` is a format string
    if (args.length == 0) return errorMessage;

    var formatter = new MessageFormat(errorMessage, locale);
    return formatter.format(args);
  }
}

import org.pkl.parser.Parser;
import org.pkl.parser.ParserError;

public class TestShebangValidation {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Parser parser = new Parser();
        
        // Test 1: Shebang at beginning (should work)
        System.out.println("Test 1: Shebang at beginning (expected: success)");
        String code1 = "#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\nfoo = 1";
        try {
            parser.parseModule(code1);
            System.out.println("✓ PASSED: Parsed successfully");
        } catch (ParserError e) {
            System.out.println("✗ FAILED: " + e.getMessage());
        }
        
        // Test 2: Shebang after code (should fail)
        System.out.println("\nTest 2: Shebang after code (expected: fail)");
        String code2 = "foo = 1\n#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval";
        try {
            parser.parseModule(code2);
            System.out.println("✗ FAILED: Should have thrown an error");
        } catch (ParserError e) {
            System.out.println("✓ PASSED: Failed as expected - " + e.getMessage());
        }
        
        // Test 3: Shebang in middle (should fail)
        System.out.println("\nTest 3: Shebang in middle (expected: fail)");
        String code3 = "foo = 1\n#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\nbar = 2";
        try {
            parser.parseModule(code3);
            System.out.println("✗ FAILED: Should have thrown an error");
        } catch (ParserError e) {
            System.out.println("✓ PASSED: Failed as expected - " + e.getMessage());
        }
        
        // Test 4: Empty file with shebang (should work)
        System.out.println("\nTest 4: Empty file with shebang (expected: success)");
        String code4 = "#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\n";
        try {
            parser.parseModule(code4);
            System.out.println("✓ PASSED: Empty module parsed successfully");
        } catch (ParserError e) {
            System.out.println("✗ FAILED: " + e.getMessage());
        }
        
        System.out.println("\n=== Complete ===");
    }
}

+import org.pkl.parser.Parser;
+import org.pkl.parser.ParserError;
+
+public class TestShebang {
+    public static void main(String[] args) {
+        Parser parser = new Parser();
+        
+        // Test case 1: Shebang at the beginning (should work)
+        String code1 = "#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\nfoo = 1";
+        System.out.println("Test 1 - Shebang at beginning:");
+        try {
+            parser.parseModule(code1);
+            System.out.println("✓ Parsed successfully (expected)");
+        } catch (ParserError e) {
+            System.out.println("✗ Failed to parse: " + e.getMessage());
+        }
+        
+        // Test case 2: Shebang after code (should fail)
+        String code2 = "foo = 1\n#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval";
+        System.out.println("\nTest 2 - Shebang after code:");
+        try {
+            parser.parseModule(code2);
+            System.out.println("✗ Parsed successfully (should have failed)");
+        } catch (ParserError e) {
+            System.out.println("✓ Failed to parse as expected: " + e.getMessage());
+        }
+        
+        // Test case 3: Shebang in the middle (should fail)
+        String code3 = "foo = 1\n#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\nbar = 2";
+        System.out.println("\nTest 3 - Shebang in the middle:");
+        try {
+            parser.parseModule(code3);
+            System.out.println("✗ Parsed successfully (should have failed)");
+        } catch (ParserError e) {
+            System.out.println("✓ Failed to parse as expected: " + e.getMessage());
+        }
+    }

+import org.pkl.parser.Parser;
+
+public class TestShebangParsing {
+    public static void main(String[] args) {
+        try {
+            Parser parser = new Parser();
+            
+            // Test 1: Shebang at beginning (should work)
+            System.out.println("Test 1: Shebang at beginning");
+            String code1 = "#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\nfoo = 1";
+            try {
+                parser.parseModule(code1);
+                System.out.println("PASS: Parsed successfully (expected)");
+            } catch (Exception e) {
+                System.out.println("FAIL: Unexpected error: " + e.getMessage());
+            }
+            
+            // Test 2: Shebang after code (should fail with fix)
+            System.out.println("\nTest 2: Shebang after code");
+            String code2 = "foo = 1\n#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval";
+            try {
+                parser.parseModule(code2);
+                System.out.println("FAIL: Should have failed parsing");
+            } catch (Exception e) {
+                System.out.println("PASS: Failed as expected: " + e.getMessage());
+            }
+            
+            // Test 3: Shebang in middle (should fail with fix)
+            System.out.println("\nTest 3: Shebang in middle");
+            String code3 = "foo = 1\n#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\nbar = 2";
+            try {
+                parser.parseModule(code3);
+                System.out.println("FAIL: Should have failed parsing");
+            } catch (Exception e) {
+                System.out.println("PASS: Failed as expected: " + e.getMessage());
+            }
+            
+            // Test 4: Multiple shebangs
+            System.out.println("\nTest 4: Multiple shebangs");
+            String code4 = "#!/bin/bash\n#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\nfoo = 1";
+            try {
+                parser.parseModule(code4);
+                System.out.println("FAIL: Should have failed parsing");
+            } catch (Exception e) {
+                System.out.println("PASS: Failed as expected: " + e.getMessage());
+            }
+            
+        } catch (Exception e) {
+            e.printStackTrace();
+        }
+    }

+import org.pkl.parser.Parser;
+import org.pkl.parser.ParserError;
+
+public class TestShebangValidation {
+    public static void main(String[] args) {
+        Parser parser = new Parser();
+        
+        // Test 1: Shebang at beginning (should work)
+        System.out.println("Test 1: Shebang at beginning (expected: success)");
+        String code1 = "#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\nfoo = 1";
+        try {
+            parser.parseModule(code1);
+            System.out.println("✓ PASSED: Parsed successfully");
+        } catch (ParserError e) {
+            System.out.println("✗ FAILED: " + e.getMessage());
+        }
+        
+        // Test 2: Shebang after code (should fail)
+        System.out.println("\nTest 2: Shebang after code (expected: fail)");
+        String code2 = "foo = 1\n#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval";
+        try {
+            parser.parseModule(code2);
+            System.out.println("✗ FAILED: Should have thrown an error");
+        } catch (ParserError e) {
+            System.out.println("✓ PASSED: Failed as expected - " + e.getMessage());
+        }
+        
+        // Test 3: Shebang in middle (should fail)
+        System.out.println("\nTest 3: Shebang in middle (expected: fail)");
+        String code3 = "foo = 1\n#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\nbar = 2";
+        try {
+            parser.parseModule(code3);
+            System.out.println("✗ FAILED: Should have thrown an error");
+        } catch (ParserError e) {
+            System.out.println("✓ PASSED: Failed as expected - " + e.getMessage());
+        }
+        
+        // Test 4: Empty file with shebang (should work)
+        System.out.println("\nTest 4: Empty file with shebang (expected: success)");
+        String code4 = "#!/usr/bin/env pkl eval\n";
+        try {
+            parser.parseModule(code4);
+            System.out.println("✓ PASSED: Empty module parsed successfully");
+        } catch (ParserError e) {
+            System.out.println("✗ FAILED: " + e.getMessage());
+        }
+        
+        System.out.println("\n=== Complete ===");
+    }
+}

+#!/bin/bash
+echo "=== Analyzing the parser structure ==="
+
+# Find where shebang tokens are skipped
+echo "1. Where SHEBANG tokens are ignored:"
+grep -n -B5 -A5 "SHEBANG" pkl-parser/src/main/java/org/pkl/parser/Parser.java
